\DoxyCodeLine{00025\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ A\ C++\ interface\ to\ gnuplot.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00026\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Web\ page:\ http://www.stahlke.org/dan/gnuplot-\/iostream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00027\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Documentation:\ https://github.com/dstahlke/gnuplot-\/iostream/wiki}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00028\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00029\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ whole\ library\ consists\ of\ this\ monolithic\ header\ file,\ for\ ease\ of\ installation\ (the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00030\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Makefile\ and\ *.cc\ files\ are\ only\ for\ examples\ and\ tests).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00031\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00032\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ TODO:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00033\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ What\ version\ of\ boost\ is\ currently\ required?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00034\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ Callbacks\ via\ gnuplot's\ 'bind'\ function.\ \ This\ would\ allow\ triggering\ user\ functions\ when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00035\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ keys\ are\ pressed\ in\ the\ gnuplot\ window.\ \ However,\ it\ would\ require\ a\ PTY\ reader\ thread.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00036\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ Maybe\ temporary\ files\ read\ in\ a\ thread\ can\ replace\ PTY\ stuff.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00037\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00038\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00140\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ MSVC\ gives\ a\ warning\ saying\ that\ fopen\ and\ getenv\ are\ not\ secure.\ \ But\ they\ are\ secure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00141\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Unfortunately\ their\ replacement\ functions\ are\ not\ simple\ drop-\/in\ replacements.\ \ The\ best}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00142\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ solution\ is\ to\ just\ temporarily\ disable\ this\ warning\ whenever\ fopen\ or\ getenv\ is\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00143\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ http://stackoverflow.com/a/4805353/1048959}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ "{}pgnuplot"{}\ is\ considered\ deprecated\ according\ to\ the\ Internet.\ \ It\ may\ be\ faster.\ \ It}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ doesn't\ seem\ to\ handle\ binary\ data\ though.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{comment}{//\#\ define\ GNUPLOT\_DEFAULT\_COMMAND\ "{}pgnuplot\ -\/persist"{}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00278\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \{\{\{1\ Feedback\ helper\ classes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00279\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00280\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Used\ for\ reading\ stuff\ sent\ from\ gnuplot\ via\ gnuplot's\ "{}print"{}\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00281\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00282\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ For\ example,\ this\ is\ used\ for\ capturing\ mouse\ clicks\ in\ the\ gnuplot\ window.\ \ There\ are\ two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00283\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ implementations,\ only\ the\ first\ of\ which\ is\ complete.\ \ The\ first\ implementation\ allocates\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00284\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ PTY\ (pseudo\ terminal)\ which\ is\ written\ to\ by\ gnuplot\ and\ read\ by\ us.\ \ This\ only\ works\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00285\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Linux.\ \ The\ second\ implementation\ creates\ a\ temporary\ file\ which\ is\ written\ to\ by\ gnuplot}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00286\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ read\ by\ us.\ \ However,\ this\ doesn't\ currently\ work\ since\ fscanf\ doesn't\ block.\ \ It\ would}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00287\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ be\ possible\ to\ get\ this\ working\ using\ a\ more\ complicated\ mechanism\ (select\ or\ threads)\ but\ I}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00288\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ haven't\ had\ the\ need\ for\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00289\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00412\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00413\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \{\{\{1\ Traits\ and\ printers\ for\ entry\ datatypes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00414\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00415\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ section\ contains\ the\ mechanisms\ for\ sending\ scalar\ and\ tuple\ data\ to\ gnuplot.\ \ Pairs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00416\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ tuples\ are\ sent\ by\ appealing\ to\ the\ senders\ defined\ for\ their\ component\ scalar\ types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00417\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Senders\ for\ arrays\ are\ defined\ in\ a\ later\ section.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00418\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00419\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ There\ are\ three\ classes\ which\ need\ to\ be\ specialized\ for\ each\ supported\ datatype:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00420\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 1.\ TextSender\ to\ send\ data\ as\ text.\ \ The\ default\ is\ to\ just\ send\ using\ the\ ostream's\ \`{}<<`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00421\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ operator.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00422\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 2.\ BinarySender\ to\ send\ data\ as\ binary,\ in\ a\ format\ which\ gnuplot\ can\ understand.\ \ There\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00423\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ no\ default\ implementation\ (unimplemented\ types\ raise\ a\ compile\ time\ error),\ however}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00424\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ inheriting\ from\ FlatBinarySender\ will\ send\ the\ data\ literally\ as\ it\ is\ stored\ in\ memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00425\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ suffices\ for\ most\ of\ the\ standard\ built-\/in\ types\ (e.g.\ uint32\_t\ or\ double).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00426\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 3.\ BinfmtSender\ sends\ a\ description\ of\ the\ data\ format\ to\ gnuplot\ (e.g.\ \`{}\%uint32`).\ \ Type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00427\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}show\ datafile\ binary\ datasizes`\ in\ gnuplot\ to\ see\ a\ list\ of\ supported\ formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00428\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00429\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \{\{\{2\ Basic\ entry\ datatypes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00430\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00431\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Default\ TextSender,\ sends\ data\ using\ \`{}<<`\ operator.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00432\ \textcolor{keyword}{template}\ <\textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ T,\ \textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ Enable=\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}>}

\DoxyCodeLine{00449\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ which\ can\ be\ sent\ this\ way\ can\ have\ their\ BinarySender\ specialization\ inherit\ from\ this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00450\ \textcolor{keyword}{template}\ <\textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ T>}

\DoxyCodeLine{00466\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ BinfmtSender\ implementations\ for\ basic\ data\ types\ supported\ by\ gnuplot.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00467\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Types\ from\ boost/cstdint.hpp\ are\ used\ because\ VS2008\ doesn't\ have\ stdint.h.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00742\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00743\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \{\{\{1\ ArrayTraits\ and\ Range\ classes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00744\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00745\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ section\ handles\ sending\ of\ array\ data\ to\ gnuplot.\ \ It\ is\ rather\ complicated\ because\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00746\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ the\ diversity\ of\ storage\ schemes\ supported.\ \ For\ example,\ it\ treats\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00747\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}std::pair<std::vector<T>,\ std::vector<U>>`\ in\ the\ same\ way\ as\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00748\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}std::vector<std::pair<T,\ U>>`,\ iterating\ through\ the\ two\ arrays\ in\ lockstep,\ and\ sending}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00749\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ pairs\ <T,U>\ to\ gnuplot\ as\ columns.\ \ In\ fact,\ any\ nested\ combination\ of\ pairs,\ tuples,\ STL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00750\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ containers,\ Blitz\ arrays,\ and\ Armadillo\ arrays\ is\ supported\ (with\ the\ caveat\ that,\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00751\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ instance,\ Blitz\ arrays\ should\ never\ be\ put\ into\ an\ STL\ container\ or\ you\ will\ suffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00752\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ unpredictable\ results\ due\ the\ way\ Blitz\ handles\ assignment).\ \ Nested\ containers\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00753\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ considered\ to\ be\ multidimensional\ arrays.\ \ Although\ gnuplot\ only\ supports\ 1D\ and\ 2D\ arrays,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00754\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ our\ module\ is\ in\ principle\ not\ limited.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00755\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00756\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ ArrayTraits\ class\ is\ specialized\ for\ every\ supported\ array\ or\ container\ type\ (the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00757\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ default,\ unspecialized,\ version\ of\ ArrayTraits\ exists\ only\ to\ tell\ you\ that\ something\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00758\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *not*\ a\ container,\ via\ the\ is\_container\ flag).\ \ ArrayTraits\ tells\ you\ the\ depth\ of\ a\ nested}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00759\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (or\ multidimensional)\ container,\ as\ well\ as\ the\ value\ type,\ and\ provides\ a\ specialized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00760\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ sort\ of\ iterator\ (a.k.a.\ "{}range"{}).\ \ Ranges\ are\ sort\ of\ like\ STL\ iterators,\ except\ that\ they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00761\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ have\ built-\/in\ knowledge\ of\ the\ end\ condition\ so\ you\ don't\ have\ to\ carry\ around\ both\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00762\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ begin()\ and\ an\ end()\ iterator\ like\ in\ STL.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00763\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00764\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ As\ an\ example\ of\ how\ this\ works,\ consider\ a\ std::pair\ of\ std::vectors.\ \ Ultimately\ this\ gets}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00765\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ sent\ to\ gnuplot\ as\ two\ columns,\ so\ the\ two\ vectors\ need\ to\ be\ iterated\ in\ lockstep.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00766\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ \`{}value\_type`\ of\ \`{}std::pair<std::vector<T>,\ std::vector<U>>`\ is\ then\ \`{}std::pair<T,\ U>`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00767\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ this\ is\ what\ deferencing\ the\ range\ (iterator)\ gives.\ \ Internally,\ this\ range\ is\ built}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00768\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ out\ of\ a\ pair\ of\ ranges\ (PairOfRange\ class),\ the\ \`{}inc()`\ (advance\ to\ next\ element)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00769\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ method\ calls\ \`{}inc()`\ on\ each\ of\ the\ children,\ and\ \`{}deref()`\ calls\ \`{}deref()`\ on\ each\ child}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00770\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ and\ combines\ the\ results\ to\ return\ a\ \`{}std::pair`.\ \ Tuples\ are\ handled\ as\ nested\ pairs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00771\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00772\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ In\ addition\ to\ PairOfRange,\ there\ is\ also\ a\ VecOfRange\ class\ that\ can\ be\ used\ to\ treat\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00773\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ outermost\ part\ of\ a\ nested\ container\ as\ if\ it\ were\ a\ tuple.\ \ Since\ tuples\ are\ printed\ as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00774\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ columns,\ this\ is\ like\ treating\ a\ multidimensional\ array\ as\ if\ it\ were\ column-\/major.\ \ A}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00775\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ VecOfRange\ is\ obtained\ by\ calling\ \`{}get\_columns\_range`.\ \ This\ is\ used\ by,\ for\ instance,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00776\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \`{}send1d\_colmajor`.\ \ The\ implementation\ is\ similar\ to\ that\ of\ PairOfRange.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00777\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00778\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ range,\ accessed\ via\ \`{}ArrayTraits<T>::get\_range`,\ will\ be\ of\ a\ different\ class\ depending}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00779\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ on\ T,\ and\ this\ is\ defined\ by\ the\ ArrayTraits\ specialization\ for\ T.\ \ It\ will\ always\ have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00780\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ methods\ \`{}inc()`\ to\ advance\ to\ the\ next\ element\ and\ \`{}is\_end()`\ for\ checking\ whether\ one\ has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00781\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ advanced\ past\ the\ final\ element.\ \ For\ nested\ containers,\ \`{}deref\_subiter()`\ returns\ a\ range}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00782\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ iterator\ for\ the\ next\ nesting\ level.\ \ When\ at\ the\ innermost\ level\ of\ nesting,\ \`{}deref()`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00783\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ returns\ the\ value\ of\ the\ entry\ the\ iterator\ points\ to\ (a\ scalar,\ pair,\ or\ tuple).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00784\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Only\ one\ of\ \`{}deref()`\ or\ \`{}deref\_subiter()`\ will\ be\ available,\ depending\ on\ whether\ there\ are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00785\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ deeper\ levels\ of\ nesting.\ \ The\ typedefs\ \`{}value\_type`\ and\ \`{}subiter\_type`\ tell\ the\ return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00786\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ types\ of\ these\ two\ methods.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00787\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00788\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Support\ for\ standard\ C++\ and\ boost\ containers\ and\ tuples\ of\ containers\ is\ provided\ in\ this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00789\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ section.\ \ Support\ for\ third\ party\ packages\ like\ Blitz\ and\ Armadillo\ is\ in\ a\ later\ section.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00790\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00791\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \{\{\{2\ ArrayTraits\ generic\ class\ and\ defaults}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00792\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00793\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Error\ messages\ involving\ this\ stem\ from\ treating\ something\ that\ was\ not\ a\ container\ as\ if\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00794\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ was.\ \ This\ is\ only\ here\ to\ allow\ compiliation\ without\ errors\ in\ normal\ cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00795\ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{structgnuplotio_1_1Error__WasNotContainer}{Error\_WasNotContainer}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00796\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ is\ just\ here\ to\ make\ VC++\ happy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00797\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ https://connect.microsoft.com/VisualStudio/feedback/details/777612/class-\/template-\/specialization-\/that-\/compiles-\/in-\/g-\/but-\/not-\/visual-\/c}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00798\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structgnuplotio_1_1Error__WasNotContainer_aeac5de90c903be765130fc14f85dfb00}{subiter\_type}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00799\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00800\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00801\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Error\ messages\ involving\ this\ stem\ from\ calling\ deref\ instead\ of\ deref\_subiter\ for\ a\ nested}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00802\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ container.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00803\ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{structgnuplotio_1_1Error__InappropriateDeref}{Error\_InappropriateDeref}}\ \{\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00804\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00805\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ unspecialized\ version\ of\ this\ class\ gives\ traits\ for\ things\ that\ are\ *not*\ arrays.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00806\ \textcolor{keyword}{template}\ <\textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ T,\ \textcolor{keyword}{typename}\ Enable=\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}>}
\DoxyCodeLine{00807\ \textcolor{keyword}{class\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classgnuplotio_1_1ArrayTraits}{ArrayTraits}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00808\ \textcolor{keyword}{public}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00809\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ value\ type\ of\ elements\ after\ all\ levels\ of\ nested\ containers\ have\ been\ dereferenced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00810\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structgnuplotio_1_1Error__WasNotContainer}{Error\_WasNotContainer}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classgnuplotio_1_1ArrayTraits_a3bcae12a7bf42af90f4946acc66f27e0}{value\_type}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00811\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ type\ of\ the\ range\ (a.k.a.\ iterator)\ that\ \`{}get\_range()`\ returns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00812\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structgnuplotio_1_1Error__WasNotContainer}{Error\_WasNotContainer}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classgnuplotio_1_1ArrayTraits_ae53464a5175c03deec403392b8dcb3c5}{range\_type}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{00813\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Tells\ whether\ T\ is\ in\ fact\ a\ container\ type.}}
